<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:индифферентный.html>индиффере́нтный</a> (30222)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ин<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>диф<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>фе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рента.html>ре́нт</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>индиффере́нтнее.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-индифферент-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***индустрия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:индустрия.html>индустри́я</a> (11539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индустрия.html>индустри́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">industríja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индустрия.html>индустри́и</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индустрия.html>индустри́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:индустрия.html>индустри́й</a></b>)

***иней.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́ней</a> (9246)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьnьjь</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьnьje</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьnьja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hoar-frost, rime</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*H₁eyH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́ней</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ínej</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́нея</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́неи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́неев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hoarfrost, frost, rime
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>190-</b> [1886],  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “Шуточка”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>Повести</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказ.html>расска́зы</a></cite>  | <cite>Stories and tales</cite> |  (<a href = vnd.unilang:сочинение.html>Сочине́ние</a> |  2), Saint Petersburg |  A.F. Marx |  translated as  “A Little Game”, in Katherine Tiernan O'Connor, transl., <cite>Anton Chekhov's Selected Stories</cite>, W.W. Norton, 2014, page 57:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясный.html>я́сный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:зимний.html>зи́мний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдень</a>... <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крепкий.html>кре́пок</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>трещи́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> на́деньки, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>де́ржит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:покрываться.html>покрыва́ются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:серебристый.html>серебри́стым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иней.html>и́неем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кудри.html>ку́дри</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:висок.html>виска́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушо́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верхний.html>ве́рхней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губо́й</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jásnyj, zímnij póldenʹ... Moróz krépok, treščít, i u Nádenʹki, kotóraja déržit menjá pod rúku, pokryvájutsja serebrístym <b>ínejem</b> kúdri na viskáx i pušók nad vérxnej gubój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A clear winter noonday... The frost is hard, it crackles, and Nadenka, who is holding me by the arm, has a silvery <b>glaze</b> coating the curls on her temples and the down on her upper lip.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> white hair</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:инженер.html>инжене́р</a> (1111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ingenieur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ingénieur</i>.

<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">initiieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">inkrustieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">incruster</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***иногда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a> (337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">inój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-гда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-gda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kogdá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for the origin of the last element.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inogdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sometimes, at times</li>
<li>now and then</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*(j)inъ</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>other, another, different</li>
<li>some, many a
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">inój raz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sometimes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́й</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne kto <b>inój</b>, kak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nobody else but</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иной.html>ино́е</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne što <b>inóje</b>, kak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nothing else but</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рка</a> (12243)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:марка.html>ма́рка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">inostránnaja márka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; since the 1980s.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">inomárka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иномарка.html>инома́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foreign-made car</li></ol>
